"Bring it all together with Gemini and your favorite appsGo from tons of tabs to one conversation. Gemini can now access info from new sources, starting with Maps, YouTube, Flights, and Hotels so you can bring your ideas to life easier and faster.The magic of Gemini comes to your stuffFind, summarize and get quick answers from your emails, docs & PDFs. For example, “summarize our recent college tour reservations from gmail and put them in a table with their date and time.”Learn more Opens in a new window Manage which apps Gemini connects toGemini shares information with connected apps, such as your location, to provide the most relevant response – but you control which apps Gemini connects to.Learn more Opens in a new window One conversation, many appsHowever your conversations evolve, Gemini can automatically pick a connected app – or multiple apps – to help respond to you./swarmnet\n  /public        <-- static assets\n  /src           <-- Astro pages/components\n  package.json   <-- \"astro\" + plugins + commands\n  astro.config.mjs\n  .sn\n  .gitignore/swarmnet\n  /public        <-- static assets\n  /src           <-- Astro pages/components\n  package.json   <-- \"astro\" + plugins + commands\n  astro.config.mjs\n  .sn\n  .gitignore\n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \n  \nProductivity Travel Media Learning ProductivityGitHub@GitHub Import code from public or private repositories, and ask questions about it.  Learn more  What external libraries are used in the attached code? Once you attach a GitHub repository to your prompt, Gemini can:Help developers better understand the codebaseAnswer questions about specific functionsSuggest code additions and improvementsDebug issuesGitHub cannot:Retrieve commit history, PRs, or other metadataRead a repository by including a GitHub URL in the promptWrite to a code repositoryPrompts to try: Understand code  Improve code  Generate code Google Workspace Find, summarize, and get quick info from your content in Gmail, Docs, Drive, and more. Gmail@Gmail Learn more Google Calendar@Google Calendar Learn more Google Docs@Google Docs Learn more Google Drive@Google Drive Learn more Google Keep@Google Keep Learn more Google Tasks@Google Tasks Learn more TravelGoogle Flights@Google Flights Pull in real-time flight info for intuitive, personalized travel planning  Learn more  Show me flights to Tokyo and give me ideas of things to do. How about Seoul too? Using Google Flights, Gemini can find flight info based on:Origin CityAirlineMaximum PriceMaximum number of stopsNumber of passengersMinimum/maximum length of tripSeating classOne way vs round tripGoogle Flights cannot:Book a flight for youGet alerts on saved flightsFind information about booked flightsFind flights over 11 months awaySearch for flights by airline alliancePrompts to try: Pack accordingly  Comparison shop  Plan a visit Google Hotels@Google Hotels Search hotels based on what's important to you, the same way you'd talk to a friend  Learn more  Find hotels in Phuket for a week in March and suggest a packing list Using Google Hotels, Gemini can Search for hotels based on:Location, number of nights, number of adults and dateCurrencyAmenitiesGoogle Hotels cannot:Book hotels for youCancel or update existing reservationsCheck in for youFind package deals not available through Google HotelsPrompts to try: Spring getaway  See the sights  Special long weekend Google Maps@Google Maps Tap into location-based information to bring your plans to life  Learn more  How long does it take to walk from Buckingham Palace to Big Ben in London? What about from Big Ben to Trafalgar Square? Using Google Maps, Gemini can:Find places such as business, stores, restaurants, parks and attractionsProvide you with addresses, descriptions, websites and ratings and opening hours for a placeFind directions based on mode of transport and help you avoid things like tollsUse your saved work and home locations to get directionsGoogle Maps cannot:Save your location historyUse your saved places, other than work or homeProvide live traffic updatesGet user reviews or restaurant menusPrompts to try: Tourist trek  Find something nearby  Are we there yet? MediaGoogle Photos@Google Photos Search for a specific memory or recall information directly from your photo library using Ask Photos  Learn more  Show me highlights from my last vacation @Google Photos Using the Photos extension, Gemini can:Quickly find specific photos and videos based on people, location, or a descriptionDiscover insights and information hidden in your photo galleryGet help writing text that's inspired by your photos, like caption ideas for social mediaGoogle Photos cannot:Edit your photosAdd labels, like names, to photos in your Photos appCreate new albums or edit existing onesPrompts to try: Photos from my last vacation  Find my license plate number  Write a caption YouTube@YouTube Discover YouTube videos and get answers about them  Learn more  Find videos of how to quickly get grape juice out of a wool rug Using YouTube, Gemini can:Find videos and playlists on a specific topicFind channels and shorts based on your interestsGet answers about the content of a video from a previous responseGet answers about video content by pasting a URL in the promptGet answers about about publish date, like count, length and view countYouTube cannot:Show videos from your watch history, liked videos, saved playlists, subscribed channelsSave something to a playlistAdd a commentPrompts to try: Get inspired  Help solve a problem  Research a topic YouTube Music@YouTube Music Play, search, and discover your favorite songs, artists, playlists and more  Learn more  Play songs where Beyoncé and Jay-Z feature together. Using YouTube Music, Gemini can:Play songs, albums and music videosSearch for songs by artist, genre or lyricsShow you your playlists and find others you might likeFind similar songs by the same or different artistStart a radio based on a suggested song or artistPlay music in the background for YouTube Music Premium members using an Android deviceYouTube Music cannot:Like a song or save it to a playlistSearch for songs, artists, and lyrics when asked in a language other than EnglishOperate playback and volume controls on iOS devicesPrompts to try: Search for songs  Discover music you'd love  Play a radio for any mood LearningOpenStax@OpenStax Retrieves passages from openly licensed textbooks from OpenStax.  Learn more  @OpenStax definition of a Lewis acid The OpenStax extension can:Pull in trustworthy responses based on Rice University’s OpenStax educational resourcesInclude citations and links to relevant textbook contentOpenStax cannot:Access teacher resourcesAlways give correct answers to textbook exercisesAccess textbooks outside of OpenStaxPrompts to try: @OpenStax...
